-- Table structure for table `transaction_histories`

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `transaction_histories` (
  `id` int(18) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `user_id` int(18) NOT NULL,
  `title` varchar(125) NOT NULL,
  `amount` decimal(13,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0.00',
  `created` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  `reference` varchar(125) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `type` smallint(3) unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB  DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1 AUTO_INCREMENT=16 ;

  `name` varchar(84) NOT NULL,
  `password` varchar(64) NOT NULL,
  `nric_new` varchar(18) CHARACTER SET latin1 COLLATE latin1_bin NOT NULL,
  `kin_name` varchar(84) NOT NULL,
  `relation` varchar(32) NOT NULL,
  `nric_new_kin` varchar(18) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `bank_number` varchar(32) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `bank_name` varchar(32) NOT NULL,
  `address` varchar(64) NOT NULL,
  `postcode` smallint(8) unsigned NOT NULL,
  `telephone` varchar(18) NOT NULL,
  `email` varchar(84) NOT NULL,
  `previous_insuran_company` varchar(64) NOT NULL,
  `cover_note` varchar(32) NOT NULL,
  `insuran_ncb` char(10) DEFAULT NULL,
  `road_tax` decimal(10,2) DEFAULT '0.00',
  `insuran_due_date` date NOT NULL DEFAULT '0000-00-00',
  `reg_number` varchar(10) NOT NULL,
  `owner_name` varchar(84) NOT NULL,
  `owner_nric` varchar(18) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `owner_dob` date NOT NULL DEFAULT '0000-00-00',
  `model` varchar(64) NOT NULL,
  `year_make` smallint(8) unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '1900',
  `capacity` smallint(8) unsigned NOT NULL,
  `engine_number` varchar(64) NOT NULL,
  `chasis_number` varchar(64) NOT NULL,
  `grant_serial_number` varchar(18) NOT NULL,
  `ip_address` varchar(18) NOT NULL,
  `created` timestamp NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  `payment` tinyint(1) DEFAULT '0',
  `email_verification` varchar(64) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `verified` tinyint(1) DEFAULT '0',
  `ctime` varchar(64) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `ckey` varchar(64) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `profile_image` varchar(64) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'nophoto.jpg',
  `sms_setting` tinyint(1) unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '1',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB  DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1 AUTO_INCREMENT=24 ;
